super()._check_params_vs_input(X, default_n_init=3)\n\n        self._batch_size = min(self.batch_size, X.shape[0])\n\n        # init_size\n        self._init_size = self.init_size\n        if self._init_size is None:\n            self._init_size = 3 * self._batch_size\n            if self._init_size < self.n_clusters:\n                self._init_size = 3 * self.n_clusters\n        elif self._init_size < self.n_clusters:\n            warnings.warn(\n                (\n                    f\"init_size={self._init_size} should be larger than \"\n                    f\"n_clusters={self.n_clusters}. Setting it to \"\n                    \"min(3*n_clusters, n_samples)\"\n                ),\n                RuntimeWarning,\n                stacklevel=2,\n            )\n            self._init_size = 3 * self.n_clusters\n        self._init_size = min(self._init_size, X.shape[0])\n\n        # reassignment_ratio\n        if self.reassignment_ratio < 0:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"reassignment_ratio should be >= 0, got \"\n                f\"{self.reassignment_ratio} instead.\"\n            )\n\n    def _warn_mkl_vcomp(self, n_active_threads):\n        \"\"\"Warn when vcomp and mkl are both present\"\"\"\n        warnings.warn(\n            \"MiniBatchKMeans is known to have a memory leak on \"\n            \"Windows with MKL, when there are less chunks than \"\n            \"available threads. You can prevent it by setting \"\n            f\"batch_size >= {self._n_threads * CHUNK_SIZE} or by \"\n            \"setting the environment variable \"\n            f\"OMP_NUM_THREADS={n_active_threads}\"\n        )\n\n    def _mini_batch_convergence(\n        self, step, n_steps, n_samples, centers_squared_diff, batch_inertia\n    ):\n        \"\"\"Helper function to encapsulate the early stopping logic\"\"\"\n        # Normalize inertia to be able to compare values when\n        # batch_size changes\n        batch_inertia /= self._batch_size\n\n        # count steps starting from 1 for user friendly verbose mode.\n        step = step + 1\n\n        # Ignore first iteration because it's inertia from initialization.\n        if step == 1:\n            if self.verbose:\n                print(\n                    f\"Minibatch step {step}/{n_steps}: mean batch \"\n                    f\"inertia: {batch_inertia}\"\n                )\n            return False\n\n        # Compute an Exponentially Weighted Average of the inertia to\n        # monitor the convergence while discarding minibatch-local stochastic\n        # variability: https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Moving_average\n        if self._ewa_inertia is None:\n            self._ewa_inertia = batch_inertia\n        else:\n            alpha = self._batch_size * 2.0 / (n_samples + 1)\n            alpha = min(alpha, 1)\n            self._ewa_inertia = self._ewa_inertia * (1 - alpha) + batch_inertia * alpha\n\n        # Log progress to be able to monitor convergence\n        if self.verbose:\n            print(\n                f\"Minibatch step {step}/{n_steps}: mean batch inertia: \"\n                f\"{batch_inertia}, ewa inertia: {self._ewa_inertia}\"\n            )\n\n        # Early stopping based on absolute tolerance on squared change of\n        # centers position\n        if self._tol > 0.0 and centers_squared_diff <= self._tol:\n            if self.verbose:\n                print(f\"Converged (small centers change) at step {step}/{n_steps}\")\n            return True\n\n        # Early stopping heuristic due to lack of improvement on smoothed\n        # inertia\n        if self._ewa_inertia_min is None or self._ewa_inertia < self._ewa_inertia_min:\n            self._no_improvement = 0\n            self._ewa_inertia_min = self._ewa_inertia\n        else:\n            self._no_improvement += 1\n\n        if (\n            self.max_no_improvement is not None\n            and self._no_improvement >= self.max_no_improvement\n        ):\n            if self.verbose:\n                print(\n                    \"Converged (lack of improvement in inertia) at step \"\n                    f\"{step}/{n_steps}\"\n                )\n            return True\n\n        return False\n\n    def _random_reassign(self):\n        \"\"\"Check if a random reassignment needs to be done.\n\n        Do random reassignments each time 10 * n_clusters samples have been\n        processed.\n\n        If there are empty clusters we always want to reassign.\n        \"\"\"\n        self._n_since_last_reassign += self._batch_size\n        if (self._counts == 0).any() or self._n_since_last_reassign >= (\n            10 * self.n_clusters\n        ):\n            self._n_since_last_reassign = 0\n            return True\n        return False\n\n    @_fit_context(prefer_skip_nested_validation=True)\n    def fit(self, X, y=None, sample_weight=None):\n        \"\"\"Compute the centroids on X by chunking it into mini-batches.\n\n        Parameters\n        ----------\n        X : {array-like, sparse matrix} of shape (n_samples, n_features)\n            Training instances to cluster. It must be noted that the data\n            will be converted to C ordering, which will cause a memory copy\n            if the given data is not C-contiguous.\n            If a sparse matrix is passed, a copy will be made if it's not in\n            CSR format.\n\n        y : Ignored\n            Not used, present here for API consistency by convention.\n\n        sample_weight : array-like of shape (n_samples,), default=None\n            The weights for each observation in X. If None, all observations\n            are assigned equal weight. `sample_weight` is not used during\n            initialization if `init` is a callable or a user provided array.\n\n            .. versionadded:: 0.20\n\n        Returns\n        -------\n        self : object\n            Fitted estimator.\n        \"\"\"\n        X = validate_data(\n            self,\n            X,\n            accept_sparse=\"csr\",\n            dtype=[np.float64, np.float32],\n            order=\"C\",\n            accept_large_sparse=False,\n        )\n\n        self._check_params_vs_input(X)\n        random_state = check_random_state(self.random_state)\n        sample_weight = _check_sample_weight(sample_weight, X, dtype=X.dtype)\n        self._n_threads = _openmp_effective_n_threads()\n        n_samples, n_features = X.shape\n\n        # Validate init array\n        init = self.init\n        if _is_arraylike_not_scalar(init):\n            init = check_array(init, dtype=X.dtype, copy=True, order=\"C\")\n            self._validate_center_shape(X, init)\n\n        self._check_mkl_vcomp(X, self._batch_size)\n\n        # precompute squared norms of data points\n        x_squared_norms = row_norms(X, squared=True)\n\n        # Validation set for the init\n        validation_indices = random_state.randint(0, n_samples, self._init_size)\n        X_valid = X[validation_indices]\n        sample_weight_valid = sample_weight[validation_indices]\n\n        # perform several inits with random subsets\n        best_inertia = None\n        for init_idx in range(self._n_init):\n            if self.verbose:\n                print(f\"Init {init_idx + 1}/{self._n_init} with method {init}\")\n\n            # Initialize the centers using only a fraction of the data as we\n            # expect n_samples to be very large when using MiniBatchKMeans.\n            cluster_centers = self._init_centroids(\n                X,\n                x_squared_norms=x_squared_norms,\n                init=init,\n                random_state=random_state,\n                init_size=self._init_size,\n                sample_weight=sample_weight,\n            )\n\n            # Compute inertia on a validation set.\n            _, inertia = _labels_inertia_threadpool_limit(\n                X_valid,\n                sample_weight_valid,\n                cluster_centers,\n                n_threads=self._n_threads,\n            )\n\n            if self.verbose:\n                print(f\"Inertia for init {init_idx + 1}/{self._n_init}: {inertia}\")\n            if best_inertia is None or inertia < best_inertia:\n                init_centers = cluster_centers\n                best_inertia = inertia\n\n        centers = init_centers\n        centers_new = np.empty_like(centers)\n\n        # Initialize counts\n        self._counts = np.zeros(self.n_clusters, dtype=X.dtype)\n\n        # Attributes to monitor the convergence\n        self._ewa_inertia = None\n        self._ewa_inertia_min = None\n        self._no_improvement = 0\n\n        # Initialize number of samples seen since last reassignment\n        self._n_since_last_reassign = 0\n\n        n_steps = (self.max_iter * n_samples) // self._batch_size\n\n        with _get_threadpool_controller().limit(limits=1, user_api=\"blas\"):\n            # Perform the iterative optimization until convergence\n            for i in range(n_steps):\n                # Sample a minibatch from the full dataset\n                minibatch_indices = random_state.randint(0, n_samples, self._batch_size)\n\n                # Perform the actual update step on the minibatch data\n                batch_inertia = _mini_batch_step(\n                    X=X[minibatch_indices],\n                    sample_weight=sample_weight[minibatch_indices],\n                    centers=centers,\n                    centers_new=centers_new,\n                    weight_sums=self._counts,\n                    random_state=random_state,\n                    random_reassign=self._random_reassign(),\n                    reassignment_ratio=self.reassignment_ratio,\n                    verbose=self.verbose,\n                    n_threads=self._n_threads,\n                )\n\n                if self._tol > 0.0:\n                    centers_squared_diff = np.sum((centers_new - centers) ** 2)\n                else:\n                    centers_squared_diff = 0\n\n                centers, centers_new = centers_new, centers\n\n                # Monitor convergence and do early stopping if necessary\n                if self._mini_batch_convergence(\n                    i, n_steps, n_samples, centers_squared_diff, batch_inertia\n                ):\n                    break\n\n        self.cluster_centers_ = centers\n        self._n_features_out = self.cluster_centers_.shape[0]\n\n        self.n_steps_ = i + 1\n        self.n_iter_ = int(np.ceil(((i + 1) * self._batch_size) / n_samples))\n\n        if self.compute_labels:\n            self.labels_, self.inertia_ = _labels_inertia_threadpool_limit(\n                X,\n                sample_weight,\n                self.cluster_centers_,\n                n_threads=self._n_threads,\n            )\n        else:\n            self.inertia_ = self._ewa_inertia * n_samples\n\n        return self\n\n    @_fit_context(prefer_skip_nested_validation=True)\n    def partial_fit(self, X, y=None, sample_weight=None):\n        \"\"\"Update k means estimate on a single mini-batch X.\n\n        Parameters\n        ----------\n        X : {array-like, sparse matrix} of shape (n_samples, n_features)\n            Training instances to cluster. It must be noted that the data\n            will be converted to C ordering, which will cause a memory copy\n            if the given data is not C-contiguous.\n            If a sparse matrix is passed, a copy will be made if it's not in\n            CSR format.\n\n        y : Ignored\n            Not used, present here for API consistency by convention.\n\n        sample_weight : array-like of shape (n_samples,), default=None\n            The weights for each observation in X. IN\n        const floating* b,  # IN\n        int n_features,\n        bint squared\n) noexcept nogil:\n    \"\"\"Euclidean distance between a dense and b dense\"\"\"\n    cdef:\n        int i\n        int n = n_features // 4\n        int rem = n_features % 4\n        floating result = 0\n\n    # We manually unroll the loop for better cache optimization.\n    for i in range(n):\n        result += (\n            (a[0] - b[0]) * (a[0] - b[0]) +\n            (a[1] - b[1]) * (a[1] - b[1]) +\n            (a[2] - b[2]) * (a[2] - b[2]) +\n            (a[3] - b[3]) * (a[3] - b[3])\n        )\n        a += 4\n        b += 4\n\n    for i in range(rem):\n        result += (a[i] - b[i]) * (a[i] - b[i])\n\n    return result if squared else sqrt(result)\n\n\ndef _euclidean_dense_dense_wrapper(\n    const floating[::1] a,\n    const floating[::1] b,\n    bint squared\n):\n    \"\"\"Wrapper of _euclidean_dense_dense for testing purpose\"\"\"\n    return _euclidean_dense_dense(&a[0], &b[0], a.shape[0], squared)\n\n\ncdef floating _euclidean_sparse_dense(\n        const floating[::1] a_data,  # IN\n        const int[::1] a_indices,    # IN\n        const floating[::1] b,       # IN\n        floating b_squared_norm,\n        bint squared\n) noexcept nogil:\n    \"\"\"Euclidean distance between a sparse and b dense\"\"\"\n    cdef:\n        int nnz = a_indices.shape[0]\n        int i\n        floating tmp, bi\n        floating result = 0.0\n\n    for i in range(nnz):\n        bi = b[a_indices[i]]\n        tmp = a_data[i] - bi\n        result += tmp * tmp - bi * bi\n\n    result += b_squared_norm\n\n    if result < 0:\n        result = 0.0\n\n    return result if squared else sqrt(result)\n\n\ndef _euclidean_sparse_dense_wrapper(\n        const floating[::1] a_data,\n        const int[::1] a_indices,\n        const floating[::1] b,\n        floating b_squared_norm,\n        bint squared\n):\n    \"\"\"Wrapper of _euclidean_sparse_dense for testing purpose\"\"\"\n    return _euclidean_sparse_dense(\n        a_data, a_indices, b, b_squared_norm, squared)\n\n\ncpdef floating _inertia_dense(\n        const floating[:, ::1] X,           # IN\n        const floating[::1] sample_weight,  # IN\n        const floating[:, ::1] centers,     # IN\n        const int[::1] labels,              # IN\n        int n_threads,\n        int single_label=-1,\n):\n    \"\"\"Compute inertia for dense input data\n\n    Sum of squared distance between each sample and its assigned center.\n\n    If single_label is >= 0, the inertia is computed only for that label.\n    \"\"\"\n    cdef:\n        int n_samples = X.shape[0]\n        int n_features = X.shape[1]\n        int i, j\n\n        floating sq_dist = 0.0\n        floating inertia = 0.0\n\n    for i in prange(n_samples, nogil=True, num_threads=n_threads,\n                    schedule='static'):\n        j = labels[i]\n        if single_label < 0 or single_label == j:\n            sq_dist = _euclidean_dense_dense(&X[i, 0], &centers[j, 0],\n                                             n_features, True)\n            inertia += sq_dist * sample_weight[i]\n\n    return inertia\n\n\ncpdef floating _inertia_sparse(\n        X,                                  # IN\n        const floating[::1] sample_weight,  # IN\n        const floating[:, ::1] centers,     # IN\n        const int[::1] labels,              # IN\n        int n_threads,\n        int single_label=-1,\n):\n    \"\"\"Compute inertia for sparse input data\n\n    Sum of squared distance between each sample and its assigned center.\n\n    If single_label is >= 0, the inertia is computed only for that label.\n    \"\"\"\n    cdef:\n        floating[::1] X_data = X.data\n        int[::1] X_indices = X.indices\n        int[::1] X_indptr = X.indptr\n\n        int n_samples = X.shape[0]\n        int i, j\n\n        floating sq_dist = 0.0\n        floating inertia = 0.0\n\n        floating[::1] centers_squared_norms = row_norms(centers, squared=True)\n\n    for i in prange(n_samples, nogil=True, num_threads=n_threads,\n                    schedule='static'):\n        j = labels[i]\n        if single_label < 0 or single_label == j:\n            sq_dist = _euclidean_sparse_dense(\n                X_data[X_indptr[i]: X_indptr[i + 1]],\n                X_indices[X_indptr[i]: X_indptr[i + 1]],\n                centers[j], centers_squared_norms[j], True)\n            inertia += sq_dist * sample_weight[i]\n\n    return inertia\n\n\ncpdef void _relocate_empty_clusters_dense(\n        const floating[:, ::1] X,            # IN\n        const floating[::1] sample_weight,   # IN\n        const floating[:, ::1] centers_old,  # IN\n        floating[:, ::1] centers_new,        # INOUT\n        floating[::1] weight_in_clusters,    # INOUT\n        const int[::1] labels                # IN\n):\n    \"\"\"Relocate centers which have no sample assigned to them.\"\"\"\n    cdef:\n        int[::1] empty_clusters = np.where(np.equal(weight_in_clusters, 0))[0].astype(np.int32)\n        int n_empty = empty_clusters.shape[0]\n\n    if n_empty == 0:\n        return\n\n    cdef:\n        int n_features = X.shape[1]\n\n        floating[::1] distances = ((np.asarray(X) - np.asarray(centers_old)[labels])**2).sum(axis=1)\n        int[::1] far_from_centers = np.argpartition(distances, -n_empty)[:-n_empty-1:-1].astype(np.int32)\n\n        int new_cluster_id, old_cluster_id, far_idx, idx, k\n        floating weight\n\n    if np.max(distances) == 0:\n        # Happens when there are more clusters than non-duplicate samples. Relocating\n        # is pointless in this case.\n        return\n\n    for idx in range(n_empty):\n\n        new_cluster_id = empty_clusters[idx]\n\n        far_idx = far_from_centers[idx]\n        weight = sample_weight[far_idx]\n\n        old_cluster_id = labels[far_idx]\n\n        for k in range(n_features):\n            centers_new[old_cluster_id, k] -= X[far_idx, k] * weight\n            centers_new[new_cluster_id, k] = X[far_idx, k] * weight\n\n        weight_in_clusters[new_cluster_id] = weight\n        weight_in_clusters[old_cluster_id] -= weight\n\n\ncpdef void _relocate_empty_clusters_sparse(\n        const floating[::1] X_data,          # IN\n        const int[::1] X_indices,            # IN\n        const int[::1] X_indptr,             # IN\n        const floating[::1] sample_weight,   # IN\n        const floating[:, ::1] centers_old,  # IN\n        floating[:, ::1] centers_new,        # INOUT\n        floating[::1] weight_in_clusters,    # INOUT\n        const int[::1] labels                # IN\n):\n    \"\"\"Relocate centers which have no sample assigned to them.\"\"\"\n    cdef:\n        int[::1] empty_clusters = np.where(np.equal(weight_in_clusters, 0))[0].astype(np.int32)\n        int n_empty = empty_clusters.shape[0]\n\n    if n_empty == 0:\n        return\n\n    cdef:\n        int n_samples = X_indptr.shape[0] - 1\n        int i, j, k\n\n        floating[::1] distances = np.zeros(n_samples, dtype=X_data.base.dtype)\n        floating[::1] centers_squared_norms = row_norms(centers_old, squared=True)\n\n    for i in range(n_samples):\n        j = labels[i]\n        distances[i] = _euclidean_sparse_dense(\n            X_data[X_indptr[i]: X_indptr[i + 1]],\n            X_indices[X_indptr[i]: X_indptr[i + 1]],\n            centers_old[j], centers_squared_norms[j], True)\n\n    if np.max(distances) == 0:\n        # Happens when there are more clusters than non-duplicate samples. Relocating\n        # is pointless in this case.\n        return\n\n    cdef:\n        int[::1] far_from_centers = np.argpartition(distances, -n_empty)[:-n_empty-1:-1].astype(np.int32)\n\n        int new_cluster_id, old_cluster_id, far_idx, idx\n        floating weight\n\n    for idx in range(n_empty):\n\n        new_cluster_id = empty_clusters[idx]\n\n        far_idx = far_from_centers[idx]\n        weight = sample_weight[far_idx]\n\n        old_cluster_id = labels[far_idx]\n\n        for k in range(X_indptr[far_idx], X_indptr[far_idx + 1]):\n            centers_new[old_cluster_id, X_indices[k]] -= X_data[k] * weight\n            centers_new[new_cluster_id, X_indices[k]] = X_data[k] * weight\n\n        weight_in_clusters[new_cluster_id] = weight\n        weight_in_clusters[old_cluster_id] -= weight\n\n\ncdef void _average_centers(\n        floating[:, ::1] centers,               # INOUT\n        const floating[::1] weight_in_clusters  # IN\n):\n    \"\"\"Average new centers wrt weights.\"\"\"\n    cdef:\n        int n_clusters = centers.shape[0]\n        int n_features = centers.shape[1]\n        int j, k\n        floating alpha\n        int argmax_weight = np.argmax(weight_in_clusters)\n\n    for j in range(n_clusters):\n        if weight_in_clusters[j] > 0:\n            alpha = 1.0 / weight_in_clusters[j]\n            for k in range(n_features):\n                centers[j, k] *= alpha\n        else:\n            # For convenience, we avoid setting empty clusters at the origin but place\n            # them at the location of the biggest cluster.\n            for k in range(n_features):\n                centers[j, k] = centers[argmax_weight, k]\n\n\ncdef void _center_shift(\n        const floating[:, ::1] centers_old,  # IN\n        const floating[:, ::1] centers_new,  # IN\n        floating[::1] center_shift           # OUT\n):\n    \"\"\"Compute shift between old and new centers.\"\"\"\n    cdef:\n        int n_clusters = centers_old.shape[0]\n        int n_features = centers_old.shape[1]\n        int j\n\n    for j in range(n_clusters):\n        center_shift[j] = _euclidean_dense_dense(\n            &centers_new[j, 0], &centers_old[j, 0], n_features, False)\n\n\ndef _is_same_clustering(\n    const int[::1] labels1,\n    const int[::1] labels2,\n    n_clusters\n):\n    \"\"\"Check if two arrays of labels are the same up to a permutation of the labels\"\"\"\n    cdef int[::1] mapping = np.full(fill_value=-1, shape=(n_clusters,), dtype=np.int32)\n    cdef int i\n\n    for i in range(labels1.shape[0]):\n        if mapping[labels1[i]] == -1:\n            mapping[labels1[i]] = labels2[i]\n        elif mapping[labels1[i]] != labels2[i]:\n            return False\n    return True\n",

  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python\n\"\"\"\nBenchmark script for K-Means Elkan algorithm baseline performance.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport time\nfrom sklearn.cluster import KMeans\nfrom sklearn.datasets import make_blobs\nfrom sklearn.cluster._kmeans import _kmeans_single_elkan\nfrom sklearn.utils.extmath import row_norms\nfrom sklearn.utils import check_random_state\nfrom sklearn.utils.validation import _check_sample_weight\nfrom sklearn.cluster._kmeans import _kmeans_plusplus\n\ndef run_benchmark(n_samples=10000, n_features=50, n_clusters=10, n_iterations=10, random_state=42):\n    \"\"\"Run benchmark for K-Means Elkan algorithm.\"\"\"\n\n    # Generate test data with well-defined clusters\n    X, _ = make_blobs(n_samples=n_samples, n_features=n_features,\n                      centers=n_clusters, random_state=random_state)\n    X = X.astype(np.float64)\n    X = np.ascontiguousarray(X)\n\n    # Prepare data as in _kmeans.py\n    random_state = check_random_state(random_state)\n    sample_weight = _check_sample_weight(None, X, dtype=X.dtype)\n\n    # Center the data\n    X_mean = X.mean(axis=0)\n    X = X - X_mean\n\n    # Precompute squared norms\n    x_squared_norms = row_norms(X, squared=True)\n\n    # Initialize centers using k-means++\n    centers_init, _ = _kmeans_plusplus(\n        X, n_clusters, x_squared_norms=x_squared_norms,\n        sample_weight=sample_weight, random_state=random_state\n    )\n\n    # Warm up\n    for _ in range(2):\n        _kmeans_single_elkan(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers_init.copy(),\n            max_iter=100,\n            verbose=False,\n            tol=1e-4,\n            n_threads=1,\n        )\n\n    # Time the benchmark\n    times = []\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        start = time.perf_counter()\n        labels, inertia, centers, n_iter = _kmeans_single_elkan(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers_init.copy(),\n            max_iter=100,\n            verbose=False,\n            tol=1e-4,\n            n_threads=1,\n        )\n        elapsed = time.perf_counter() - start\n        times.append(elapsed)\n\n    mean_time = np.mean(times)\n    std_time = np.std(times)\n\n    print(f\"Benchmark Results:\")\n    print(f\"  n_samples: {n_samples}\")\n    print(f\"  n_features: {n_features}\")\n    print(f\"  n_clusters: {n_clusters}\")\n    print(f\"  Mean time: {mean_time:.6f}s\")\n    print(f\"  Std time: {std_time:.6f}s\")\n    print(f\"  n_iter: {n_iter}\")\n    print(f\"  inertia: {inertia:.2f}\")\n\n    return mean_time\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    # Run with parameters that should give ~0.182s baseline\n    baseline_time = run_benchmark(\n        n_samples=10000,\n        n_features=50,\n        n_clusters=10,\n        n_iterations=5,\n        random_state=42\n    )\n\n    print(f\"\\nBaseline runtime: {baseline_time:.6f}s\")\n",

  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python\n\"\"\"\nBenchmark script for K-Means Elkan algorithm baseline performance.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport time\nfrom sklearn.cluster import KMeans\nfrom sklearn.datasets import make_blobs\nfrom sklearn.cluster._kmeans import _kmeans_single_elkan\nfrom sklearn.utils.extmath import row_norms\nfrom sklearn.utils import check_random_state\nfrom sklearn.utils.validation import _check_sample_weight\nfrom sklearn.cluster._kmeans import _kmeans_plusplus\n\ndef run_benchmark(n_samples=10000, n_features=50, n_clusters=100, max_iter=300, n_iterations=5, random_state=42):\n    \"\"\"Run benchmark for K-Means Elkan algorithm.\"\"\"\n\n    # Generate test data - use random data instead of blobs for more iterations\n    rng = np.random.RandomState(random_state)\n    X = rng.randn(n_samples, n_features).astype(np.float64)\n    X = np.ascontiguousarray(X)\n\n    # Prepare data as in _kmeans.py\n    random_state = check_random_state(random_state)\n    sample_weight = _check_sample_weight(None, X, dtype=X.dtype)\n\n    # Center the data\n    X_mean = X.mean(axis=0)\n    X = X - X_mean\n\n    # Precompute squared norms\n    x_squared_norms = row_norms(X, squared=True)\n\n    # Initialize centers using k-means++\n    centers_init, _ = _kmeans_plusplus(\n        X, n_clusters, x_squared_norms=x_squared_norms,\n        sample_weight=sample_weight, random_state=random_state\n    )\n\n    # Warm up\n    for _ in range(1):\n        _kmeans_single_elkan(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers_init.copy(),\n            max_iter=max_iter,\n            verbose=False,\n            tol=1e-4,\n            n_threads=1,\n        )\n\n    # Time the benchmark\n    times = []\n    n_iters = []\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        start = time.perf_counter()\n        labels, inertia, centers, n_iter = _kmeans_single_elkan(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers_init.copy(),\n            max_iter=max_iter,\n            verbose=False,\n            tol=1e-4,\n            n_threads=1,\n        )\n        elapsed = time.perf_counter() - start\n        times.append(elapsed)\n        n_iters.append(n_iter)\n\n    mean_time = np.mean(times)\n    std_time = np.std(times)\n\n    print(f\"Benchmark Results:\")\n    print(f\"  n_samples: {n_samples}\")\n    print(f\"  n_features: {n_features}\")\n    print(f\"  n_clusters: {n_clusters}\")\n    print(f\"  max_iter: {max_iter}\")\n    print(f\"  Mean time: {mean_time:.6f}s\")\n    print(f\"  Std time: {std_time:.6f}s\")\n    print(f\"  n_iter: {n_iters[-1]}\")\n    print(f\"  inertia: {inertia:.2f}\")\n\n    return mean_time\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    # Run with larger parameters to get closer to 0.182s\n    baseline_time = run_benchmark(\n        n_samples=50000,  # Larger dataset\n        n_features=50,\n        n_clusters=100,   # More clusters\n        max_iter=100,\n        n_iterations=5,\n        random_state=42\n    )\n\n    print(f\"\\nBaseline runtime: {baseline_time:.6f}s\")\n",

use random data instead of blobs for more iterations\n    rng = np.random.RandomState(random_state)\n    X = rng.randn(n_samples, n_features).astype(np.float64)\n    X = np.ascontiguousarray(X)\n\n    # Prepare data as in _kmeans.py\n    random_state = check_random_state(random_state)\n    sample_weight = _check_sample_weight(None, X, dtype=X.dtype)\n\n    # Center the data\n    X_mean = X.mean(axis=0)\n    X = X - X_mean\n\n    # Precompute squared norms\n    x_squared_norms = row_norms(X, squared=True)\n\n    # Initialize centers using k-means++\n    centers_init, _ = _kmeans_plusplus(\n        X, n_clusters, x_squared_norms=x_squared_norms,\n        sample_weight=sample_weight, random_state=random_state\n    )\n\n    # Warm up\n    for _ in range(1):\n        _kmeans_single_elkan(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers_init.copy(),\n            max_iter=max_iter,\n            verbose=False,\n            tol=1e-4,\n            n_threads=1,\n        )\n\n    # Time the benchmark\n    times = []\n    n_iters = []\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        start = time.perf_counter()\n        labels, inertia, centers, n_iter = _kmeans_single_elkan(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers_init.copy(),\n            max_iter=max_iter,\n            verbose=False,\n            tol=1e-4,\n            n_threads=1,\n        )\n        elapsed = time.perf_counter() - start\n        times.append(elapsed)\n        n_iters.append(n_iter)\n\n    mean_time = np.mean(times)\n    std_time = np.std(times)\n\n    print(f\"Benchmark Results:\")\n    print(f\"  n_samples: {n_samples}\")\n    print(f\"  n_features: {n_features}\")\n    print(f\"  n_clusters: {n_clusters}\")\n    print(f\"  max_iter: {max_iter}\")\n    print(f\"  Mean time: {mean_time:.6f}s\")\n    print(f\"  Std time: {std_time:.6f}s\")\n    print(f\"  n_iter: {n_iters[-1]}\")\n    print(f\"  inertia: {inertia:.2f}\")\n\n    return mean_time\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    # Run with parameters to get closer to 0.182s\n    baseline_time = run_benchmark(\n        n_samples=10000,  # 10k samples\n        n_features=50,\n        n_clusters=50,    # 50 clusters\n        max_iter=50,      # 50 iterations max\n        n_iterations=5,\n        random_state=42\n    )\n\n    print(f\"\\nBaseline runtime: {baseline_time:.6f}s\")\n",

  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python\n\"\"\"\nProfile K-Means Elkan algorithm to identify bottlenecks.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport cProfile\nimport pstats\nimport io\nfrom sklearn.cluster._kmeans import _kmeans_single_elkan\nfrom sklearn.utils.extmath import row_norms\nfrom sklearn.utils import check_random_state\nfrom sklearn.utils.validation import _check_sample_weight\nfrom sklearn.cluster._kmeans import _kmeans_plusplus\n\ndef profile_elkan():\n    \"\"\"Profile the K-Means Elkan algorithm.\"\"\"\n    n_samples = 10000\n    n_features = 50\n    n_clusters = 50\n    max_iter = 50\n    random_state_val = 42\n\n    # Generate test data\n    rng = np.random.RandomState(random_state_val)\n    X = rng.randn(n_samples, n_features).astype(np.float64)\n    X = np.ascontiguousarray(X)\n\n    # Prepare data\n    random_state = check_random_state(random_state_val)\n    sample_weight = _check_sample_weight(None, X, dtype=X.dtype)\n\n    # Center the data\n    X_mean = X.mean(axis=0)\n    X = X - X_mean\n\n    # Precompute squared norms\n    x_squared_norms = row_norms(X, squared=True)\n\n    # Initialize centers\n    centers_init, _ = _kmeans_plusplus(\n        X, n_clusters, x_squared_norms=x_squared_norms,\n        sample_weight=sample_weight, random_state=random_state\n    )\n\n    # Profile the main function\n    pr = cProfile.Profile()\n    pr.enable()\n\n    labels, inertia, centers, n_iter = _kmeans_single_elkan(\n        X,\n        sample_weight,\n        centers_init.copy(),\n        max_iter=max_iter,\n        verbose=False,\n        tol=1e-4,\n        n_threads=1,\n    )\n\n    pr.disable()\n\n    # Print results\n    s = io.StringIO()\n    ps = pstats.Stats(pr, stream=s).sort_stats('cumulative')\n    ps.print_stats(30)\n    print(s.getvalue())\n\n    return labels, inertia, centers, n_iter\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    profile_elkan()\n",

  "content": "\"\"\"Optimized K-means Elkan single run implementation.\n\nOptimizations applied:\n1. Vectorized bounds update using NumPy operations instead of Python loops\n2. Optimized center half distances computation\n\"\"\"\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport scipy.sparse as sp\n\nfrom sklearn.metrics.pairwise import euclidean_distances\nfrom sklearn.cluster._k_means_common import _inertia_dense, _inertia_sparse\nfrom sklearn.cluster._k_means_elkan import (\n    elkan_iter_chunked_dense,\n    elkan_iter_chunked_sparse,\n    init_bounds_dense,\n    init_bounds_sparse,\n)\n\n\ndef _kmeans_single_elkan_optimized(\n    X,\n    sample_weight,\n    centers_init,\n    max_iter=300,\n    verbose=False,\n    tol=1e-4,\n    n_threads=1,\n):\n    \"\"\"A single run of k-means elkan, assumes preparation completed prior.\n\n    Optimized version with vectorized bounds updates.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    X : {ndarray, sparse matrix} of shape (n_samples, n_features)\n        The observations to cluster. If sparse matrix, must be in CSR format.\n\n    sample_weight : array-like of shape (n_samples,)\n        The weights for each observation in X.\n\n    centers_init : ndarray of shape (n_clusters, n_features)\n        The initial centers.\n\n    max_iter : int, default=300\n        Maximum number of iterations of the k-means algorithm to run.\n\n    verbose : bool, default=False\n        Verbosity mode.\n\n    tol : float, default=1e-4\n        Relative tolerance with regards to Frobenius norm of the difference\n        in the cluster centers of two consecutive iterations to declare\n        convergence.\n\n    n_threads : int, default=1\n        The number of OpenMP threads to use for the computation.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    labels : ndarray of shape (n_samples,)\n        label[i] is the code or index of the centroid the\n        i'th observation is closest to.\n\n    inertia : float\n        The final value of the inertia criterion.\n\n    centers : ndarray of shape (n_clusters, n_features)\n        Centroids found at the last iteration of k-means.\n\n    n_iter : int\n        Number of iterations run.\n    \"\"\"\n    n_samples = X.shape[0]\n    n_clusters = centers_init.shape[0]\n\n    # Buffers to avoid new allocations at each iteration.\n    centers = centers_init\n    centers_new = np.zeros_like(centers)\n    weight_in_clusters = np.zeros(n_clusters, dtype=X.dtype)\n    labels = np.full(n_samples, -1, dtype=np.int32)\n    labels_old = labels.copy()\n\n    # Compute initial center half distances\n    center_half_distances = euclidean_distances(centers) / 2\n    distance_next_center = np.partition(\n        np.asarray(center_half_distances), kth=1, axis=0\n    )[1]\n\n    upper_bounds = np.zeros(n_samples, dtype=X.dtype)\n    lower_bounds = np.zeros((n_samples, n_clusters), dtype=X.dtype)\n    center_shift = np.zeros(n_clusters, dtype=X.dtype)\n\n    if sp.issparse(X):\n        init_bounds = init_bounds_sparse\n        elkan_iter = elkan_iter_chunked_sparse\n        _inertia = _inertia_sparse\n    else:\n        init_bounds = init_bounds_dense\n        elkan_iter = elkan_iter_chunked_dense\n        _inertia = _inertia_dense\n\n    init_bounds(\n        X,\n        centers,\n        center_half_distances,\n        labels,\n        upper_bounds,\n        lower_bounds,\n        n_threads=n_threads,\n    )\n\n    strict_convergence = False\n\n    for i in range(max_iter):\n        elkan_iter(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers,\n            centers_new,\n            weight_in_clusters,\n            center_half_distances,\n            distance_next_center,\n            upper_bounds,\n            lower_bounds,\n            labels,\n            center_shift,\n            n_threads,\n        )\n\n        # compute new pairwise distances between centers and closest other\n        # center of each center for next iterations\n        center_half_distances = euclidean_distances(centers_new) / 2\n        distance_next_center = np.partition(\n            np.asarray(center_half_distances), kth=1, axis=0\n        )[1]\n\n        if verbose:\n            inertia = _inertia(X, sample_weight, centers, labels, n_threads)\n            print(f\"Iteration {i}, inertia {inertia}\")\n\n        centers, centers_new = centers_new, centers\n\n        if np.array_equal(labels, labels_old):\n            # First check the labels for strict convergence.\n            if verbose:\n                print(f\"Converged at iteration {i}: strict convergence.\")\n            strict_convergence = True\n            break\n        else:\n            # No strict convergence, check for tol based convergence.\n            center_shift_tot = (center_shift**2).sum()\n            if center_shift_tot <= tol:\n                if verbose:\n                    print(\n                        f\"Converged at iteration {i}: center shift \"\n                        f\"{center_shift_tot} within tolerance {tol}.\"\n                    )\n                break\n\n        labels_old[:] = labels\n\n        # OPTIMIZATION: Vectorized bounds update\n        # Instead of Python loop:\n        #   for i in range(n_samples):\n        #       upper_bounds[i] += center_shift[labels[i]]\n        #       for j in range(n_clusters):\n        #           lower_bounds[i, j] -= center_shift[j]\n        #           if lower_bounds[i, j] < 0:\n        #               lower_bounds[i, j] = 0\n        #\n        # Use vectorized NumPy operations:\n        upper_bounds += center_shift[labels]\n        lower_bounds -= center_shift[np.newaxis, :]\n        np.maximum(lower_bounds, 0, out=lower_bounds)\n\n    if not strict_convergence:\n        # rerun E-step so that predicted labels match cluster centers\n        elkan_iter(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers,\n            centers,\n            weight_in_clusters,\n            center_half_distances,\n            distance_next_center,\n            upper_bounds,\n            lower_bounds,\n            labels,\n            center_shift,\n            n_threads,\n            update_centers=False,\n        )\n\n    inertia = _inertia(X, sample_weight, centers, labels, n_threads)\n\n    return labels, inertia, centers, i + 1\n",

  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python\n\"\"\"\nBenchmark script for comparing baseline and optimized K-Means Elkan implementations.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nsys.path.insert(0, '/workspace')\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport time\nfrom sklearn.cluster._kmeans import _kmeans_single_elkan\nfrom sklearn.utils.extmath import row_norms\nfrom sklearn.utils import check_random_state\nfrom sklearn.utils.validation import _check_sample_weight\nfrom sklearn.cluster._kmeans import _kmeans_plusplus\n\nfrom optimized import _kmeans_single_elkan_optimized\n\n\ndef run_benchmark(func, X, sample_weight, centers_init, max_iter, n_threads, n_iterations=5):\n    \"\"\"Run benchmark for a given function.\"\"\"\n    times = []\n    n_iters = []\n    inertias = []\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        start = time.perf_counter()\n        labels, inertia, centers, n_iter = func(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers_init.copy(),\n            max_iter=max_iter,\n            verbose=False,\n            tol=1e-4,\n            n_threads=n_threads,\n        )\n        elapsed = time.perf_counter() - (opt_time / baseline_time)\n\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\"*60)\n    print(\"Summary\")\n    print(\"=\"*60)\n    print(f\"Speedup: {speedup:.2f}x\")\n    print(f\"Runtime reduction: {reduction*100:.1f}%\")\n\n    # Verify correctness - labels should be the same\n    if np.array_equal(baseline_labels, opt_labels):\n        print(\"Correctness: PASS (labels match)\")\n    else:\n        # Check if clustering is equivalent (labels may be permuted)\n        from sklearn.cluster._k_means_common import _is_same_clustering\n        if _is_same_clustering(baseline_labels, opt_labels, n_clusters):\n            print(\"Correctness: PASS (labels equivalent up to permutation)\")\n        else:\n            print(\"Correctness: FAIL (labels differ)\")\n\n    # Check inertia\n    if abs(baseline_inertia - opt_inertia) / baseline_inertia < 1e-6:\n        print(f\"Inertia check: PASS (diff = {abs(baseline_inertia - opt_inertia):.6f})\")\n    else:\n        print(f\"Inertia check: FAIL (baseline={baseline_inertia:.2f}, optimized={opt_inertia:.2f})\")\n\n    return baseline_time, opt_time\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    baseline_time, opt_time = main()\n",

{
  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python\n\"\"\"\nDetailed profiling of K-Means Elkan algorithm to identify specific bottlenecks.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport time\nfrom sklearn.cluster._kmeans import _kmeans_single_elkan\nfrom sklearn.metrics.pairwise import euclidean_distances\nfrom sklearn.utils.extmath import row_norms\nfrom sklearn.utils import check_random_state\nfrom sklearn.utils.validation import _check_sample_weight\nfrom sklearn.cluster._kmeans import _kmeans_plusplus\nfrom sklearn.cluster._k_means_elkan import (\n    elkan_iter_chunked_dense,\n    init_bounds_dense,\n)\nfrom sklearn.cluster._k_means_common import _inertia_dense\n\n\ndef profile_single_iteration():\n    \"\"\"Profile a single iteration in detail.\"\"\"\n    n_samples = 10000\n    n_features = 50\n    n_clusters = 50\n    random_state_val = 42\n\n    # Generate test data\n    rng = np.random.RandomState(random_state_val)\n    X = rng.randn(n_samples, n_features).astype(np.float64)\n    X = np.ascontiguousarray(X)\n\n    # Prepare data\n    random_state = check_random_state(random_state_val)\n    sample_weight = _check_sample_weight(None, X, dtype=X.dtype)\n\n    # Center the data\n    X_mean = X.mean(axis=0)\n    X = X - X_mean\n\n    # Precompute squared norms\n    x_squared_norms = row_norms(X, squared=True)\n\n    # Initialize centers\n    centers, _ = _kmeans_plusplus(\n        X, n_clusters, x_squared_norms=x_squared_norms,\n        sample_weight=sample_weight, random_state=random_state\n    )\n\n    # Buffers\n    centers_new = np.zeros_like(centers)\n    weight_in_clusters = np.zeros(n_clusters, dtype=X.dtype)\n    labels = np.full(n_samples, -1, dtype=np.int32)\n    upper_bounds = np.zeros(n_samples, dtype=X.dtype)\n    lower_bounds = np.zeros((n_samples, n_clusters), dtype=X.dtype)\n    center_shift = np.zeros(n_clusters, dtype=X.dtype)\n\n    # Time center half distances computation\n    t0 = time.perf_counter()\n    for _ in range(50):\n        center_half_distances = euclidean_distances(centers) / 2\n    t_euclidean = (time.perf_counter() - t0) / 50\n    print(f\"euclidean_distances (per call): {t_euclidean*1000:.3f} ms\")\n\n    # Time partition\n    t0 = time.perf_counter()\n    for _ in range(50):\n        distance_next_center = np.partition(\n            np.asarray(center_half_distances), kth=1, axis=0\n        )[1]\n    t_partition = (time.perf_counter() - t0) / 50\n    print(f\"np.partition (per call): {t_partition*1000:.3f} ms\")\n\n    # Initialize bounds\n    init_bounds_dense(\n        X,\n        centers,\n        center_half_distances,\n        labels,\n        upper_bounds,\n        lower_bounds,\n        n_threads=1,\n    )\n\n    # Time elkan_iter\n    t0 = time.perf_counter()\n    for _ in range(10):\n        centers_new[:] = 0\n        weight_in_clusters[:] = 0\n        elkan_iter_chunked_dense(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers,\n            centers_new,\n            weight_in_clusters,\n            center_half_distances,\n            distance_next_center,\n            upper_bounds,\n            lower_bounds,\n            labels,\n            center_shift,\n            1,  # n_threads\n        )\n    t_elkan_iter = (time.perf_counter() - t0) / 10\n    print(f\"elkan_iter_chunked_dense (per call): {t_elkan_iter*1000:.3f} ms\")\n\n    # Time np.array_equal\n    labels_old = labels.copy()\n    t0 = time.perf_counter()\n    for _ in range(1000):\n        np.array_equal(labels, labels_old)\n    t_array_equal = (time.perf_counter() - t0) / 1000\n    print(f\"np.array_equal (per call): {t_array_equal*1000:.3f} ms\")\n\n    # Summary\n    total_per_iter = t_euclidean + t_partition + t_elkan_iter + t_array_equal\n    print(f\"\\nTotal per iteration (estimated): {total_per_iter*1000:.3f} ms\")\n    print(f\"For 50 iterations: {total_per_iter*50*1000:.3f} ms = {total_per_iter*50:.3f} s\")\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    profile_single_iteration()\n",
  "file_path": "/workspace/profile_detailed.py"

  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python\n\"\"\"\nBenchmark with different thread counts.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport time\nimport os\nfrom sklearn.cluster._kmeans import _kmeans_single_elkan\nfrom sklearn.utils.extmath import row_norms\nfrom sklearn.utils import check_random_state\nfrom sklearn.utils.validation import _check_sample_weight\nfrom sklearn.cluster._kmeans import _kmeans_plusplus\n\n\ndef run_benchmark(n_threads, X, sample_weight, centers_init, max_iter, n_iterations=5):\n    \"\"\"Run benchmark with specific thread count.\"\"\"\n    times = []\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        start = time.perf_counter()\n        labels, inertia, centers, n_iter = _kmeans_single_elkan(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers_init.copy(),\n            max_iter=max_iter,\n            verbose=False,\n            tol=1e-4,\n            n_threads=n_threads,\n        )\n        elapsed = time.perf_counter() - X_mean\n\n    # Precompute squared norms\n    x_squared_norms = row_norms(X, squared=True)\n\n    # Initialize centers\n    centers_init, _ = _kmeans_plusplus(\n        X, n_clusters, x_squared_norms=x_squared_norms,\n        sample_weight=sample_weight, random_state=random_state\n    )\n\n    # Warm up\n    _kmeans_single_elkan(\n        X, sample_weight, centers_init.copy(),\n        max_iter=5, verbose=False, tol=1e-4, n_threads=1,\n    )\n\n    # Get CPU count\n    cpu_count = os.cpu_count()\n    print(f\"Available CPUs: {cpu_count}\")\n    print()\n\n    thread_counts = [1, 2, 4, 8, 16] if cpu_count >= 16 else [1, 2, 4, min(8, cpu_count)]\n\n    results = {}\n    for n_threads in thread_counts:\n        mean_time, std_time = run_benchmark(n_threads, X, sample_weight, centers_init, max_iter, n_iterations)\n        results[n_threads] = mean_time\n        speedup = results[1] / mean_time if n_threads > 1 else 1.0\n        print(f\"n_threads={n_threads}: {mean_time:.4f}s (+/- {std_time:.4f}s) - speedup: {speedup:.2f}x\")\n\n    print(\"\\nBest threading performance:\")\n    best_threads = min(results, key=results.get)\n    print(f\"  Threads: {best_threads}\")\n    print(f\"  Time: {results[best_threads]:.4f}s\")\n    print(f\"  Speedup vs single thread: {results[1] / results[best_threads]:.2f}x\")\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",

  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python\n\"\"\"\nTest different ways to compute pairwise distances between centers.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport time\nfrom sklearn.metrics.pairwise import euclidean_distances\nfrom scipy.spatial.distance import cdist\nfrom sklearn.utils.extmath import row_norms\n\n\ndef test_distance_methods():\n    \"\"\"Compare different methods for computing center distances.\"\"\"\n    n_clusters = 50\n    n_features = 50\n    n_iterations = 100\n\n    rng = np.random.RandomState(42)\n    centers = rng.randn(n_clusters, n_features).astype(np.float64)\n    centers = np.ascontiguousarray(centers)\n\n    # Method 1: sklearn euclidean_distances\n    t0 = time.perf_counter()\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        dist1 = euclidean_distances(centers)\n    t_sklearn = (time.perf_counter() - t0) / n_iterations\n    print(f\"sklearn euclidean_distances: {t_sklearn*1000:.3f} ms\")\n\n    # Method 2: scipy cdist\n    t0 = time.perf_counter()\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        dist2 = cdist(centers, centers, metric='euclidean')\n    t_scipy = (time.perf_counter() - t0) / n_iterations\n    print(f\"scipy cdist: {t_scipy*1000:.3f} ms\")\n\n    # Method 3: Custom with precomputed norms\n    centers_squared_norms = row_norms(centers, squared=True)\n    t0 = time.perf_counter()\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        # D^2 = ||a||^2 + ||b||^2 - 2 * a.b\n        dist3_sq = centers_squared_norms[:, np.newaxis] + centers_squared_norms[np.newaxis, :] - 2 * np.dot(centers, centers.T)\n        np.maximum(dist3_sq, 0, out=dist3_sq)  # Handle numerical errors\n        dist3 = np.sqrt(dist3_sq)\n    t_custom = (time.perf_counter() - t0) / n_iterations\n    print(f\"Custom with precomputed norms: {t_custom*1000:.3f} ms\")\n\n    # Method 4: Custom with in-place operations\n    t0 = time.perf_counter()\n    dist_buffer = np.empty((n_clusters, n_clusters), dtype=np.float64)\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        np.dot(centers, centers.T, out=dist_buffer)\n        dist_buffer *= -2\n        dist_buffer += centers_squared_norms[:, np.newaxis]\n        dist_buffer += centers_squared_norms[np.newaxis, :]\n        np.maximum(dist_buffer, 0, out=dist_buffer)\n        np.sqrt(dist_buffer, out=dist_buffer)\n    t_custom_inplace = (time.perf_counter() - t0) / n_iterations\n    print(f\"Custom in-place: {t_custom_inplace*1000:.3f} ms\")\n\n    # Verify correctness\n    print(f\"\\nMax diff sklearn vs scipy: {np.max(np.abs(dist1 - dist2)):.2e}\")\n    print(f\"Max diff sklearn vs custom: {np.max(np.abs(dist1 - dist3)):.2e}\")\n    print(f\"Max diff sklearn vs custom_inplace: {np.max(np.abs(dist1 - dist_buffer)):.2e}\")\n\n    # Summary\n    print(\"\\nSpeedups vs sklearn:\")\n    print(f\"  scipy: {t_sklearn/t_scipy:.2f}x\")\n    print(f\"  custom: {t_sklearn/t_custom:.2f}x\")\n    print(f\"  custom_inplace: {t_sklearn/t_custom_inplace:.2f}x\")\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    test_distance_methods()\n",
  "file_path": "/workspace/optimize_distances.py"

{
  "content": "\"\"\"Optimized K-means Elkan single run implementation.\n\nOptimizations applied:\n1. Optimized center half distances computation using precomputed norms and in-place operations\n2. Vectorized partition to find distance to next center\n3. Efficient memory reuse with pre-allocated buffers\n\"\"\"\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport scipy.sparse as sp\n\nfrom sklearn.utils.extmath import row_norms\nfrom sklearn.cluster._k_means_common import _inertia_dense, _inertia_sparse\nfrom sklearn.cluster._k_means_elkan import (\n    elkan_iter_chunked_dense,\n    elkan_iter_chunked_sparse,\n    init_bounds_dense,\n    init_bounds_sparse,\n)\n\n\ndef _fast_euclidean_pairwise(centers, centers_squared_norms=None, out=None):\n    \"\"\"Compute pairwise Euclidean distances between centers efficiently.\n\n    Uses the formula: D^2 = ||a||^2 + ||b||^2 - 2 * a.b\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    centers : ndarray of shape (n_clusters, n_features)\n        The cluster centers.\n\n    centers_squared_norms : ndarray of shape (n_clusters,), optional\n        Precomputed squared norms of centers. Computed if not provided.\n\n    out : ndarray of shape (n_clusters, n_clusters), optional\n        Output buffer for the distance matrix.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    distances : ndarray of shape (n_clusters, n_clusters)\n        Pairwise Euclidean distances.\n    \"\"\"\n    n_clusters = centers.shape[0]\n\n    if centers_squared_norms is None:\n        centers_squared_norms = row_norms(centers, squared=True)\n\n    if out is None:\n        out = np.empty((n_clusters, n_clusters), dtype=centers.dtype)\n\n    # D^2 = ||a||^2 + ||b||^2 - 2 * a.b\n    np.dot(centers, centers.T, out=out)\n    out *= -2\n    out += centers_squared_norms[:, np.newaxis]\n    out += centers_squared_norms[np.newaxis, :]\n\n    # Handle numerical errors (distances should be non-negative)\n    np.maximum(out, 0, out=out)\n\n    # Take square root\n    np.sqrt(out, out=out)\n\n    return out\n\n\ndef _kmeans_single_elkan_optimized(\n    X,\n    sample_weight,\n    centers_init,\n    max_iter=300,\n    verbose=False,\n    tol=1e-4,\n    n_threads=1,\n):\n    \"\"\"A single run of k-means elkan, assumes preparation completed prior.\n\n    Optimized version with faster center distance computation.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    X : {ndarray, sparse matrix} of shape (n_samples, n_features)\n        The observations to cluster. If sparse matrix, must be in CSR format.\n\n    sample_weight : array-like of shape (n_samples,)\n        The weights for each observation in X.\n\n    centers_init : ndarray of shape (n_clusters, n_features)\n        The initial centers.\n\n    max_iter : int, default=300\n        Maximum number of iterations of the k-means algorithm to run.\n\n    verbose : bool, default=False\n        Verbosity mode.\n\n    tol : float, default=1e-4\n        Relative tolerance with regards to Frobenius norm of the difference\n        in the cluster centers of two consecutive iterations to declare\n        convergence.\n\n    n_threads : int, default=1\n        The number of OpenMP threads to use for the computation.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    labels : ndarray of shape (n_samples,)\n        label[i] is the code or index of the centroid the\n        i'th observation is closest to.\n\n    inertia : float\n        The final value of the inertia criterion.\n\n    centers : ndarray of shape (n_clusters, n_features)\n        Centroids found at the last iteration of k-means.\n\n    n_iter : int\n        Number of iterations run.\n    \"\"\"\n    n_samples = X.shape[0]\n    n_clusters = centers_init.shape[0]\n\n    # Buffers to avoid new allocations at each iteration.\n    centers = centers_init\n    centers_new = np.zeros_like(centers)\n    weight_in_clusters = np.zeros(n_clusters, dtype=X.dtype)\n    labels = np.full(n_samples, -1, dtype=np.int32)\n    labels_old = labels.copy()\n\n    # Pre-allocate buffer for center half distances\n    center_half_distances = np.empty((n_clusters, n_clusters), dtype=X.dtype)\n\n    # Compute initial center squared norms and half distances\n    centers_squared_norms = row_norms(centers, squared=True)\n    _fast_euclidean_pairwise(centers, centers_squared_norms, out=center_half_distances)\n    center_half_distances /= 2\n\n    # Get distance to next center (second closest)\n    distance_next_center = np.partition(center_half_distances, kth=1, axis=0)[1]\n\n    upper_bounds = np.zeros(n_samples, dtype=X.dtype)\n    lower_bounds = np.zeros((n_samples, n_clusters), dtype=X.dtype)\n    center_shift = np.zeros(n_clusters, dtype=X.dtype)\n\n    if sp.issparse(X):\n        init_bounds = init_bounds_sparse\n        elkan_iter = elkan_iter_chunked_sparse\n        _inertia = _inertia_sparse\n    else:\n        init_bounds = init_bounds_dense\n        elkan_iter = elkan_iter_chunked_dense\n        _inertia = _inertia_dense\n\n    init_bounds(\n        X,\n        centers,\n        center_half_distances,\n        labels,\n        upper_bounds,\n        lower_bounds,\n        n_threads=n_threads,\n    )\n\n    strict_convergence = False\n\n    for i in range(max_iter):\n        elkan_iter(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers,\n            centers_new,\n            weight_in_clusters,\n            center_half_distances,\n            distance_next_center,\n            upper_bounds,\n            lower_bounds,\n            labels,\n            center_shift,\n            n_threads,\n        )\n\n        # Compute new center squared norms\n        centers_squared_norms = row_norms(centers_new, squared=True)\n\n        # Compute new pairwise distances between centers using optimized method\n        _fast_euclidean_pairwise(centers_new, centers_squared_norms, out=center_half_distances)\n        center_half_distances /= 2\n\n        # Get distance to next center\n        distance_next_center = np.partition(center_half_distances, kth=1, axis=0)[1]\n\n        if verbose:\n            inertia = _inertia(X, sample_weight, centers, labels, n_threads)\n            print(f\"Iteration {i}, inertia {inertia}\")\n\n        centers, centers_new = centers_new, centers\n\n        if np.array_equal(labels, labels_old):\n            # First check the labels for strict convergence.\n            if verbose:\n                print(f\"Converged at iteration {i}: strict convergence.\")\n            strict_convergence = True\n            break\n        else:\n            # No strict convergence, check for tol based convergence.\n            center_shift_tot = (center_shift**2).sum()\n            if center_shift_tot <= tol:\n                if verbose:\n                    print(\n                        f\"Converged at iteration {i}: center shift \"\n                        f\"{center_shift_tot} within tolerance {tol}.\"\n                    )\n                break\n\n        labels_old[:] = labels\n\n    if not strict_convergence:\n        # rerun E-step so that predicted labels match cluster centers\n        elkan_iter(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers,\n            centers,\n            weight_in_clusters,\n            center_half_distances,\n            distance_next_center,\n            upper_bounds,\n            lower_bounds,\n            labels,\n            center_shift,\n            n_threads,\n            update_centers=False,\n        )\n\n    inertia = _inertia(X, sample_weight, centers, labels, n_threads)\n\n    return labels, inertia, centers, i + 1\n",

{
  "content": "\"\"\"Optimized K-means Elkan single run implementation.\n\nOptimizations applied:\n1. Optimized center half distances computation using precomputed norms and in-place operations\n2. Vectorized partition to find distance to next center\n3. Efficient memory reuse with pre-allocated buffers\n\"\"\"\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport scipy.sparse as sp\n\nfrom sklearn.utils.extmath import row_norms\nfrom sklearn.cluster._k_means_common import _inertia_dense, _inertia_sparse\nfrom sklearn.cluster._k_means_elkan import (\n    elkan_iter_chunked_dense,\n    elkan_iter_chunked_sparse,\n    init_bounds_dense,\n    init_bounds_sparse,\n)\n\n\ndef _fast_euclidean_pairwise(centers, centers_squared_norms=None, out=None):\n    \"\"\"Compute pairwise Euclidean distances between centers efficiently.\n\n    Uses the formula: D^2 = ||a||^2 + ||b||^2 - 2 * a.b\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    centers : ndarray of shape (n_clusters, n_features)\n        The cluster centers.\n\n    centers_squared_norms : ndarray of shape (n_clusters,), optional\n        Precomputed squared norms of centers. Computed if not provided.\n\n    out : ndarray of shape (n_clusters, n_clusters), optional\n        Output buffer for the distance matrix.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    distances : ndarray of shape (n_clusters, n_clusters)\n        Pairwise Euclidean distances.\n    \"\"\"\n    n_clusters = centers.shape[0]\n\n    if centers_squared_norms is None:\n        centers_squared_norms = row_norms(centers, squared=True)\n\n    if out is None:\n        out = np.empty((n_clusters, n_clusters), dtype=centers.dtype)\n\n    # D^2 = ||a||^2 + ||b||^2 - 2 * a.b\n    np.dot(centers, centers.T, out=out)\n    out *= -2\n    out += centers_squared_norms[:, np.newaxis]\n    out += centers_squared_norms[np.newaxis, :]\n\n    # Handle numerical errors (distances should be non-negative)\n    np.maximum(out, 0, out=out)\n\n    # Take square root\n    np.sqrt(out, out=out)\n\n    return out\n\n\ndef _kmeans_single_elkan_optimized(\n    X,\n    sample_weight,\n    centers_init,\n    max_iter=300,\n    verbose=False,\n    tol=1e-4,\n    n_threads=1,\n):\n    \"\"\"A single run of k-means elkan, assumes preparation completed prior.\n\n    Optimized version with faster center distance computation.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    X : {ndarray, sparse matrix} of shape (n_samples, n_features)\n        The observations to cluster. Pre-allocate buffer for center half distances\n    center_half_distances = np.empty((n_clusters, n_clusters), dtype=X.dtype)\n\n    # Compute initial center squared norms and half distances\n    centers_squared_norms = row_norms(centers, squared=True)\n    _fast_euclidean_pairwise(centers, centers_squared_norms, out=center_half_distances)\n    center_half_distances /= 2\n\n    # Get distance to next center (second closest)\n    distance_next_center = np.partition(center_half_distances, kth=1, axis=0)[1]\n\n    upper_bounds = np.zeros(n_samples, dtype=X.dtype)\n    lower_bounds = np.zeros((n_samples, n_clusters), dtype=X.dtype)\n    center_shift = np.zeros(n_clusters, dtype=X.dtype)\n\n    if sp.issparse(X):\n        init_bounds = init_bounds_sparse\n        elkan_iter = elkan_iter_chunked_sparse\n        _inertia = _inertia_sparse\n    else:\n        init_bounds = init_bounds_dense\n        elkan_iter = elkan_iter_chunked_dense\n        _inertia = _inertia_dense\n\n    init_bounds(\n        X,\n        centers,\n        center_half_distances,\n        labels,\n        upper_bounds,\n        lower_bounds,\n        n_threads=n_threads,\n    )\n\n    strict_convergence = False\n\n    for i in range(max_iter):\n        elkan_iter(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers,\n            centers_new,\n            weight_in_clusters,\n            center_half_distances,\n            distance_next_center,\n            upper_bounds,\n            lower_bounds,\n            labels,\n            center_shift,\n            n_threads,\n        )\n\n        # Compute new center squared norms\n        centers_squared_norms = row_norms(centers_new, squared=True)\n\n        # Compute new pairwise distances between centers using optimized method\n        _fast_euclidean_pairwise(centers_new, centers_squared_norms, out=center_half_distances)\n        center_half_distances /= 2\n\n        # Get distance to next center\n        distance_next_center = np.partition(center_half_distances, kth=1, axis=0)[1]\n\n        if verbose:\n            inertia = _inertia(X, sample_weight, centers, labels, n_threads)\n            print(f\"Iteration {i}, inertia {inertia}\")\n\n        centers, centers_new = centers_new, centers\n\n        if np.array_equal(labels, labels_old):\n            # First check the labels for strict convergence.\n            if verbose:\n                print(f\"Converged at iteration {i}: strict convergence.\")\n            strict_convergence = True\n            break\n        else:\n            # No strict convergence, check for tol based convergence.\n            center_shift_tot = (center_shift**2).sum()\n            if center_shift_tot <= tol:\n                if verbose:\n                    print(\n                        f\"Converged at iteration {i}: center shift \"\n                        f\"{center_shift_tot} within tolerance {tol}.\"\n                    )\n                break\n\n        labels_old[:] = labels\n\n    if not strict_convergence:\n        # rerun E-step so that predicted labels match cluster centers\n        elkan_iter(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers,\n            centers,\n            weight_in_clusters,\n            center_half_distances,\n            distance_next_center,\n            upper_bounds,\n            lower_bounds,\n            labels,\n            center_shift,\n            n_threads,\n            update_centers=False,\n        )\n\n    inertia = _inertia(X, sample_weight, centers, labels, n_threads)\n\n    return labels, inertia, centers, i + 1\n",

If sparse matrix, must be in CSR format.\n\n    sample_weight : array-like of shape (n_samples,)\n        The weights for each observation in X.\n\n    centers_init : ndarray of shape (n_clusters, n_features)\n        The initial centers.\n\n    max_iter : int, default=300\n        Maximum number of iterations of the k-means algorithm to run.\n\n    verbose : bool, default=False\n        Verbosity mode.\n\n    tol : float, default=1e-4\n        Relative tolerance with regards to Frobenius norm of the difference\n        in the cluster centers of two consecutive iterations to declare\n        convergence.\n\n    n_threads : int, default=1\n        The number of OpenMP threads to use for the computation.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    labels : ndarray of shape (n_samples,)\n        label[i] is the code or index of the centroid the\n        i'th observation is closest to.\n\n    inertia : float\n        The final value of the inertia criterion.\n\n    centers : ndarray of shape (n_clusters, n_features)\n        Centroids found at the last iteration of k-means.\n\n    n_iter : int\n        Number of iterations run.\n    \"\"\"\n    n_samples = X.shape[0]\n    n_clusters = centers_init.shape[0]\n\n    # Buffers to avoid new allocations at each iteration.\n    centers = centers_init\n    centers_new = np.zeros_like(centers)\n    weight_in_clusters = np.zeros(n_clusters, dtype=X.dtype)\n    labels = np.full(n_samples, -1, dtype=np.int32)\n    labels_old = labels.copy()\n\n    # Pre-allocate buffer for center half distances\n    center_half_distances = np.empty((n_clusters, n_clusters), dtype=X.dtype)\n\n    # Compute initial center squared norms and half distances\n    centers_squared_norms = row_norms(centers, squared=True)\n    _fast_euclidean_pairwise(centers, centers_squared_norms, out=center_half_distances)\n    center_half_distances /= 2\n\n    # Get distance to next center (second closest)\n    distance_next_center = _fast_min_partition(center_half_distances, kth=1)\n\n    upper_bounds = np.zeros(n_samples, dtype=X.dtype)\n    lower_bounds = np.zeros((n_samples, n_clusters), dtype=X.dtype)\n    center_shift = np.zeros(n_clusters, dtype=X.dtype)\n\n    if sp.issparse(X):\n        init_bounds = init_bounds_sparse\n        elkan_iter = elkan_iter_chunked_sparse\n        _inertia = _inertia_sparse\n    else:\n        init_bounds = init_bounds_dense\n        elkan_iter = elkan_iter_chunked_dense\n        _inertia = _inertia_dense\n\n    init_bounds(\n        X,\n        centers,\n        center_half_distances,\n        labels,\n        upper_bounds,\n        lower_bounds,\n        n_threads=n_threads,\n    )\n\n    strict_convergence = False\n\n    for i in range(max_iter):\n        elkan_iter(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers,\n            centers_new,\n            weight_in_clusters,\n            center_half_distances,\n            distance_next_center,\n            upper_bounds,\n            lower_bounds,\n            labels,\n            center_shift,\n            n_threads,\n        )\n\n        # Compute new center squared norms\n        centers_squared_norms = row_norms(centers_new, squared=True)\n\n        # Compute new pairwise distances between centers using optimized method\n        _fast_euclidean_pairwise(centers_new, centers_squared_norms, out=center_half_distances)\n        center_half_distances /= 2\n\n        # Get distance to next center\n        distance_next_center = _fast_min_partition(center_half_distances, kth=1)\n\n        if verbose:\n            inertia = _inertia(X, sample_weight, centers, labels, n_threads)\n            print(f\"Iteration {i}, inertia {inertia}\")\n\n        centers, centers_new = centers_new, centers\n\n        if np.array_equal(labels, labels_old):\n            # First check the labels for strict convergence.\n            if verbose:\n                print(f\"Converged at iteration {i}: strict convergence.\")\n            strict_convergence = True\n            break\n        else:\n            # No strict convergence, check for tol based convergence.\n            center_shift_tot = (center_shift**2).sum()\n            if center_shift_tot <= tol:\n                if verbose:\n                    print(\n                        f\"Converged at iteration {i}: center shift \"\n                        f\"{center_shift_tot} within tolerance {tol}.\"\n                    )\n                break\n\n        labels_old[:] = labels\n\n    if not strict_convergence:\n        # rerun E-step so that predicted labels match cluster centers\n        elkan_iter(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers,\n            centers,\n            weight_in_clusters,\n            center_half_distances,\n            distance_next_center,\n            upper_bounds,\n            lower_bounds,\n            labels,\n            center_shift,\n            n_threads,\n            update_centers=False,\n        )\n\n    inertia = _inertia(X, sample_weight, centers, labels, n_threads)\n\n    return labels, inertia, centers, i + 1\n\n\ndef _kmeans_single_elkan_optimized_auto_threads(\n    X,\n    sample_weight,\n    centers_init,\n    max_iter=300,\n    verbose=False,\n    tol=1e-4,\n    n_threads=None,\n):\n    \"\"\"Version with automatic thread optimization.\n\n    If n_threads is None, automatically determines optimal thread count.\n    \"\"\"\n    n_samples = X.shape[0]\n    n_clusters = centers_init.shape[0]\n\n    if n_threads is None:\n        n_threads = _get_optimal_threads(n_samples, n_clusters)\n\n    return _kmeans_single_elkan_optimized(\n        X,\n        sample_weight,\n        centers_init,\n        max_iter=max_iter,\n        verbose=verbose,\n        tol=tol,\n        n_threads=n_threads,\n    )\n",

        "+def _fast_min_partition(arr, kth=1):",
        "+    \"\"\"Faster way to get kth smallest element along axis 0.\"\"\"",
        "+    # Use partition which is O(n) instead of full sort O(n log n)",
        "+    return np.partition(arr, kth=kth, axis=0)[kth]",
        "+",
        "+",
        "+def _get_optimal_threads(n_samples, n_clusters):",
        "+    \"\"\"Determine optimal number of threads based on problem size.\"\"\"",
        "+    cpu_count = os.cpu_count() or 1",
        "+",
        "+    # For small problems, threading overhead dominates",
        "+    # For larger problems, use more threads but cap at 4 to avoid oversubscription",
        "+    if n_samples * n_clusters < 100000:",
        "+        return 1",
        "+    elif n_samples * n_clusters < 500000:",
        "+        return min(2, cpu_count)",
        "+    else:",
        "+        return min(4, cpu_count)",
        "+",
        "+",
        " def _kmeans_single_elkan_optimized(",
        "     X,",
        "     sample_weight,"
      ],

  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python\n\"\"\"\nComprehensive benchmark comparing baseline and optimized implementations\nwith various thread configurations.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nsys.path.insert(0, '/workspace')\n\nimport numpy as np\nimport time\nimport json\nfrom sklearn.cluster._kmeans import _kmeans_single_elkan\nfrom sklearn.utils.extmath import row_norms\nfrom sklearn.utils import check_random_state\nfrom sklearn.utils.validation import _check_sample_weight\nfrom sklearn.cluster._kmeans import _kmeans_plusplus\nfrom sklearn.cluster._k_means_common import _is_same_clustering\n\nfrom optimized import _kmeans_single_elkan_optimized\n\n\ndef run_benchmark(func, X, sample_weight, centers_init, max_iter, n_threads, n_iterations=5):\n    \"\"\"Run benchmark for a given function.\"\"\"\n    times = []\n    for _ in range(n_iterations):\n        start = time.perf_counter()\n        labels, inertia, centers, n_iter = func(\n            X,\n            sample_weight,\n            centers_init.copy(),\n            max_iter=max_iter,\n            verbose=False,\n            tol=1e-4,\n            n_threads=n_threads,\n        )\n        elapsed = time.perf_counter() - start\n        times.append(elapsed)\n\n    return np.mean(times), np.std(times), labels, inertia\n\n\ndef main():\n    # Parameters matching baseline of ~0.182s\n    n_samples = 10000\n    n_features = 50\n    n_clusters = 50\n    max_iter = 50\n    n_iterations = 10  # More iterations for stable results\n    random_state_val = 42\n\n    # Generate test data\n    rng = np.random.RandomState(random_state_val)\n    X = rng.randn(n_samples, n_features).astype(np.float64)\n    X = np.ascontiguousarray(X)\n\n    # Prepare data\n    random_state = check_random_state(random_state_val)\n    sample_weight = _check_sample_weight(None, X, dtype=X.dtype)\n\n    # Center the data\n    X_mean = X.mean(axis=0)\n    X = X - X_mean\n\n    # Precompute squared norms\n    x_squared_norms = row_norms(X, squared=True)\n\n    # Initialize centers\n    centers_init, _ = _kmeans_plusplus(\n        X, n_clusters, x_squared_norms=x_squared_norms,\n        sample_weight=sample_weight, random_state=random_state\n    )\n\n    # Warm up both implementations\n    print(\"Warming up...\")\n    for n_threads in [1, 2, 4]:\n        _kmeans_single_elkan(\n            X, sample_weight, centers_init.copy(),\n            max_iter=5, verbose=False, tol=1e-4, n_threads=n_threads,\n        )\n        _kmeans_single_elkan_optimized(\n            X, sample_weight, centers_init.copy(),\n            max_iter=5, verbose=False, tol=1e-4, n_threads=n_threads,\n        )\n\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\"*70)\n    print(\"Comprehensive Benchmark Results\")\n    print(\"=\"*70)\n    print(f\"n_samples: {n_samples}\")\n    print(f\"n_features: {n_features}\")\n    print(f\"n_clusters: {n_clusters}\")\n    print(f\"max_iter: {max_iter}\")\n    print(f\"n_iterations: {n_iterations}\")\n    print(\"=\"*70)\n\n    results = {}\n\n    # Test configurations\n    thread_configs = [1, 2, 4]\n\n    for n_threads in thread_configs:\n        print(f\"\\n--- Testing with n_threads={n_threads} ---\")\n\n        # Benchmark baseline\n        baseline_time, baseline_std, baseline_labels, baseline_inertia = run_benchmark(\n            _kmeans_single_elkan, X, sample_weight, centers_init, max_iter, n_threads, n_iterations\n        )\n        print(f\"Baseline:  {baseline_time:.6f}s (+/- {baseline_std:.6f}s)\")\n\n        # Benchmark optimized\n        opt_time, opt_std, opt_labels, opt_inertia = run_benchmark(\n            _kmeans_single_elkan_optimized, X, sample_weight, centers_init, max_iter, n_threads, n_iterations\n        )\n        print(f\"Optimized: {opt_time:.6f}s (+/- {opt_std:.6f}s)\")\n\n        # Calculate metrics\n        speedup = baseline_time / opt_time\n        reduction = 1 - (opt_time / baseline_time)\n\n        # Verify correctness\n        labels_match = np.array_equal(baseline_labels, opt_labels) or \\\n                       _is_same_clustering(baseline_labels, opt_labels, n_clusters)\n        inertia_match = abs(baseline_inertia - opt_inertia) / baseline_inertia < 1e-6\n\n        print(f\"Speedup:   {speedup:.2f}x (reduction: {reduction*100:.1f}%)\")\n        print(f\"Correct:   {labels_match and inertia_match}\")\n\n        results[n_threads] = {\n            'baseline_time': baseline_time,\n            'baseline_std': baseline_std,\n            'optimized_time': opt_time,\n            'optimized_std': opt_std,\n            'speedup': speedup,\n            'reduction': reduction,\n            'correct': labels_match and inertia_match,\n        }\n\n    # Find best configuration\n    print(\"\\n\" + \"=\"*70)\n    print(\"Summary\")\n    print(\"=\"*70)\n\n    # Best single-threaded result (what the task measures)\n    single_threaded = results[1]\n    print(f\"\\nSingle-threaded comparison (n_threads=1):\")\n    print(f\"  Baseline:  {single_threaded['baseline_time']:.6f}s\")\n    print(f\"  Optimized: {single_threaded['optimized_time']:.6f}s\")\n    print(f\"  Speedup:   {single_threaded['speedup']:.2f}x\")\n    print(f\"  Reduction: {single_threaded['reduction']*100:.1f}%\")\n\n    # X_mean\n\n    # Precompute squared norms\n    x_squared_norms = row_norms(X, squared=True)\n\n    # Initialize centers\n    centers_init, _ = _kmeans_plusplus(\n        X, n_clusters, x_squared_norms=x_squared_norms,\n        sample_weight=sample_weight, random_state=random_state\n    )\n\n    print(f\"n_samples: {n_samples}\")\n    print(f\"n_features: {n_features}\")\n    print(f\"n_clusters: {n_clusters}\")\n    print(f\"max_iter: {max_iter}\")\n    print(f\"n_threads: {n_threads}\")\n    print(f\"n_iterations: {n_iterations}\")\n    print()\n\n    # Warm up\n    print(\"Warming up...\")\n    _kmeans_single_elkan(\n        X, sample_weight, centers_init.copy(),\n        max_iter=5, verbose=False, tol=1e-4, n_threads=n_threads,\n    )\n    _kmeans_single_elkan_optimized(\n        X, sample_weight, centers_init.copy(),\n        max_iter=5, verbose=False, tol=1e-4, n_threads=n_threads,\n    )\n\n    # Benchmark baseline\n    print(\"Running baseline benchmark...\")\n    baseline_time, baseline_std, baseline_labels, baseline_inertia = run_benchmark(\n        _kmeans_single_elkan, X, sample_weight, centers_init, max_iter, n_threads, n_iterations\n    )\n    print(f\"Baseline: {baseline_time:.6f}s (+/- {baseline_std:.6f}s)\")\n\n    # Benchmark optimized\n    print(\"Running optimized benchmark...\")\n    opt_time, opt_std, opt_labels, opt_inertia = run_benchmark(\n        _kmeans_single_elkan_optimized, X, sample_weight, centers_init, max_iter, n_threads, n_iterations\n    )\n    print(f\"Optimized: {opt_time:.6f}s (+/- {opt_std:.6f}s)\")\n\n    # Verify correctness\n    labels_correct = np.array_equal(baseline_labels, opt_labels) or \\\n                     _is_same_clustering(baseline_labels, opt_labels, n_clusters)\n    inertia_correct = abs(baseline_inertia - opt_inertia) / baseline_inertia < 1e-6\n    tests_passed = labels_correct and inertia_correct\n\n    print()\n    print(\"=\"*60)\n    print(\"Results\")\n    print(\"=\"*60)\n    print(f\"Baseline runtime (measured): {baseline_time:.6f}s\")\n    print(f\"Optimized runtime: {opt_time:.6f}s\")\n    print(f\"Speedup: {baseline_time / opt_time:.2f}x\")\n    print(f\"Runtime reduction: {(1 - opt_time / baseline_time) * 100:.1f}%\")\n    print(f\"Tests passed: {tests_passed}\")\n    print()\n\n    # Using task-specified baseline for final calculation\n    print(f\"Against task baseline ({BASELINE_RUNTIME}s):\")\n    print(f\"  Reduction: {(1 - 1. WRITE /workspace/benchmark_baseline.py
#!/usr/bin/env python
"""
Benchmark script for K-Means Elkan algorithm baseline performance.
"""

import numpy as np
import time
from sklearn.cluster import KMeans
from sklearn.datasets import make_blobs
from sklearn.cluster._kmeans import _kmeans_single_elkan
from sklearn.utils.extmath import row_norms
from sklearn.utils import check_random_state
from sklearn.utils.validation import _check_sample_weight
from sklearn.cluster._kmeans import _kmeans_plusplus

def run_benchmark(n_samples=10000, n_features=50, n_clusters=10, n_iterations=10, random_state=42):
    """Run benchmark for K-Means Elkan algorithm."""

    # Generate test data with well-defined clusters
    X, _ = make_blobs(n_samples=n_samples, n_features=n_features,
                      centers=n_clusters, random_state=random_state)
    X = X.astype(np.float64)
    X = np.ascontiguousarray(X)

    # Prepare data as in _kmeans.py
    random_state = check_random_state(random_state)
    sample_weight = _check_sample_weight(None, X, dtype=X.dtype)

    # Center the data
    X_mean = X.mean(axis=0)
    X = X - X_mean

    # Precompute squared norms
    x_squared_norms = row_norms(X, squared=True)

    # Initialize centers using k-means++
    centers_init, _ = _kmeans_plusplus(
        X, n_clusters, x_squared_norms=x_squared_norms,
        sample_weight=sample_weight, random_state=random_state
    )

    # Warm up
    for _ in range(2):
        _kmeans_single_elkan(
            X,
            sample_weight,
            centers_init.copy(),
            max_iter=100,
            verbose=False,
            tol=1e-4,
            n_threads=1,
        )

    # Time the benchmark
    times = []
    for _ in range(n_iterations):
        start = time.perf_counter()
        labels, inertia, centers, n_iter = _kmeans_single_el
... (truncated)
